<div
class="header
artist_info_header
int-1
clearfix">














<h1
class="hed-1"
title="All-American
Rejects"
itemprop="name">All-American
Rejects</h1>














<div
class="header_btns">















<div
class="bookmark"
data-musicid="R6460"></div>














</div>













</div>













<div
class="int-1">














<div
class="content_right">















<div
class="artist_bio_container
clearfix">
















<div
class="artist_bio
short_bio">
















<div
class="artist_bio_inner">

















Vocalist/bassist
Tyson
Ritter
and
guitarist
Nick
Wheeler
both
hail
from
Stillwater,
OK,
where
the
pair
first
embraced
music
as
an
appealing
diversion
from
the
ho-hum
life
of
small-town
America.
Citing
such
influences
as


















<a
href="/ac-dc"
class="hash">AC/DC</a>,


















<a
href="/def-leppard"
class="hash">Def
Leppard</a>,
and


















<a
href="/bon-jovi"
class="hash">Bon
Jovi</a>,
they
formed
the
emo-pop
group
All-American
Rejects
in
2000,
while
both
members
were
still
in
high
school.
Maintaining
a
full
lineup
proved
to
be
difficult,
however,
so
Ritter
and
Wheeler
employed
drum
loops
and
pre-programmed
rhythm
tracks
during
their
early
performances,
an
arrangement
they
then
reprised
on
their
self-titled
debut.
Originally
released
on
the
Doghouse
label
in
October
2002,
the
poppy
record
was
later
reissued
to
a
national
audience
by
DreamWorks.
The
band
scored
a
hit
with
the
effervescent
single
&quot;Swing,
Swing,&quot;
which
attracted
attention
from
Interscope
Records
and
ultimately
landed
the
All-American
Rejects
on
the
label's
prized
roster.


















<br
/>

















<br
/>


















<a
href="/all-american-rejects/move-along"
class="hash">Move
Along</a>,
the
band's
sophomore
album
(and
first
for
Interscope),
was
released
in
July
2005;
it
also
marked
the
official
debut
of
Mike
Kennerty
(guitar)
and
Chris
Gaylor
(drums),
both
of
whom
had
joined
the
band
in
2002
after
the
completion
of
the
Rejects'
eponymous
debut.
Like
its
predecessor,


















<a
href="/all-american-rejects/move-along"
class="hash">Move
Along</a>
went
platinum,
with
three
singles
(&quot;Dirty
Little
Secret,&quot;
&quot;Move
Along,&quot;
and
&quot;It
Ends
Tonight&quot;)
enjoying
chart
success
in
the
U.S.
and
abroad.
Recording
sessions
for
a
third
album
commenced
in
mid-2007
and
ran
through
the
following
year,
causing
the
All-American
Rejects
to
cancel
their
scheduled
Warped
Tour
performances
(as
well
as
a
string
of
shows
with


















<a
href="/simple-plan"
class="hash">Simple
Plan</a>).


















<a
href="/all-american-rejects/when-world-comes-down"
class="hash">When
the
World
Comes
Down</a>
ultimately
arrived
in
December
2008,
preceded
by
the
single
&quot;Gives
You
Hell.&quot;
The
band
hit
the
road
in
support
of
the
album,
but
were
forced
to
cut
their
tour
short
in
2009
after
Ritter
was
confined
to
a
wheelchair
after
getting
knee
surgery.
The
band
got
back
to
writing
the
following
year,
working
with
producer
Greg
Wells
on
their
fourth
album,
Kids
in
the
Street,
which
arrived
in
2012.
~
Andrew
Leahey,
Rovi
















</div>















</div>
















<a
href="#"
class="full_bio_link">full
bio</a>















</div>

<script

One
Gift

apply
to

One

One

(\"Purchaser\")

Subscription
online
or
by
purchasing
a
Pandora
One
Gift
Card
and
transferring

to

(\"Recipient\").
The

and

in

Pandora
is

		<li>To

Subscription

must
provide
valid
registration
information,
a
valid
payment

at

time
of
purchase.

purchasing
a
Pandora
One
Gift
Subscription,
you
authorize
Pandora
to
charge
the
purchase
price
of
the
Pandora
One
Gift
Subscription,
and
any
applicable
sales,
telecommunication,

to
the

that

provide.</li>
		<li>The
Purchaser
is
not
entitled
to
a

or
credit
for
any
reason,
including,
without

if
the
Recipient

to

the
Pandora
One
Gift
Subscription,

required
by

a

One
Gift

Pandora
One
Gift

prior

Pandora
One
Gift
Subscription
online

for

		<li>The
Purchaser
may
not
transfer
a
single
Pandora
One
Gift
Subscription
to
more
than
one
recipient.
A
Pandora
One
Gift
Subscription
is
fully
transferable
by
the
Recipient
prior
to
activation
or

In

event

by

or

Pandora
One

		<li>Recipients
may

Pandora
One
Gift
Subscriptions
at
